dengan 5-Fold CV\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-46-cell-6-training-function-dengan-5-fold-cv\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: 4.6 Cell 6: Training Function dengan 5-Fold CV\" href=\"#46-cell-6-training-function-dengan-5-fold-cv\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"def train_and_evaluate_cv(X, y, model, model_name, n_splits=5):\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    Train model dengan 5-Fold Stratified Cross Validation\n    dan hitung metrics + training time\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    # Setup 5-Fold Stratified Cross Validation\n    skf = StratifiedKFold(n_splits=n_splits, shuffle=True, random_state=42)\n    \n    # Define scorers\n    scorers = {\n        'accuracy': make_scorer(accuracy_score),\n        'precision': make_scorer(precision_score, average='binary'),\n        'recall': make_scorer(recall_score, average='binary'),\n        'f1': make_scorer(f1_score, average='binary')\n    }\n    \n    # Start training timer\n    start_time = time.time()\n    \n    # Perform cross validation\n    cv_results = cross_validate(\n        model, X, y, \n        cv=skf, \n        scoring=scorers,\n        return_train_score=False,\n        n_jobs=-1\n    )\n    \n    # End training timer\n    training_time = time.time() - start_time\n    \n    # Calculate mean metrics across all folds\n    metrics = {\n        'accuracy': cv_results['test_accuracy'].mean(),\n        'accuracy_std': cv_results['test_accuracy'].std(),\n        'precision': cv_results['test_precision'].mean(),\n        'precision_std': cv_results['test_precision'].std(),\n        'recall': cv_results['test_recall'].mean(),\n        'recall_std': cv_results['test_recall'].std(),\n        'f1': cv_results['test_f1'].mean(),\n        'f1_std': cv_results['test_f1'].std(),\n        'training_time': training_time\n    }\n    \n    return metrics\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003edef\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003etrain_and_evaluate_cv\u003c/span\u003e(\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003eX\u003c/span\u003e, \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003ey\u003c/span\u003e, \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003emodel\u003c/span\u003e, \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003emodel_name\u003c/span\u003e, \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003en_splits\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e5\u003c/span\u003e):\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"\"\"\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e    Train model dengan 5-Fold Stratified Cross Validation\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e    dan hitung metrics + training time\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e    \"\"\"\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# Setup 5-Fold Stratified Cross Validation\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eskf\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eStratifiedKFold\u003c/span\u003e(\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003en_splits\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003en_splits\u003c/span\u003e, \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eshuffle\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003eTrue\u003c/span\u003e, \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003erandom_state\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e42\u003c/span\u003e)\n    \n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# Define scorers\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003escorers\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e {\n        \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e'accuracy'\u003c/span\u003e: \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003emake_scorer\u003c/span\u003e(\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eaccuracy_score\u003c/span\u003e),\n        \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e'precision'\u003c/span\u003e: \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003emake_scorer\u003c/span\u003e(\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eprecision_score\u003c/span\u003e, \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eaverage\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e'binary'\u003c/span\u003e),\n        \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e'recall'\u003c/span\u003e: \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003emake_scorer\u003c/span\u003e(\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003erecall_score\u003c/span\u003e, \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eaverage\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e'binary'\u003c/span\u003e),\n        \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e'f1'\u003c/span\u003e: \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003emake_scorer\u003c/span\u003e(\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003ef1_score\u003c/span\u003e, \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eaverage\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    if n_features \u0026lt;= 10:\n        max_depth = 10  # Untuk top 10 features\n    else:\n        max_depth = 20  # Untuk all features (53)\n    \n    return {\n ini\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e4\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eTop 10 hanya -0.05% dari All Features\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eFeature selection sangat worth <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Deteksi Phishing URL dengan Machine Learning</h2><a id="user-content-deteksi-phishing-url-dengan-machine-learning" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Deteksi Phishing URL dengan Machine Learning" href="#deteksi-phishing-url-dengan-machine-learning"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">1. PENDAHULUAN</h1><a id="user-content-1-pendahuluan" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 1. PENDAHULUAN" href="#1-pendahuluan"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">1.1 Latar Belakang</h2><a id="user-content-11-latar-belakang" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 1.1 Latar Belakang" href="#11-latar-belakang"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Phishing adalah serangan siber yang menipu pengguna untuk memberikan informasi sensitif melalui situs web palsu yang menyerupai situs asli. Deteksi otomatis URL phishing menggunakan <strong>Machine Learning</strong> menjadi solusi penting untuk melindungi pengguna internet.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">1.2 Tujuan Eksperimen</h2><a id="user-content-12-tujuan-eksperimen" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 1.2 Tujuan Eksperimen" href="#12-tujuan-eksperimen"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Eksperimen ini bertujuan untuk:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Membandingkan 4 metode Feature Selection</strong> untuk memilih fitur terbaik dari 53 fitur</li>
<li><strong>Mengevaluasi 3 model klasifikasi</strong> (Random Forest, XGBoost/GradientBoosting, SVM)</li>
<li><strong>Menganalisis trade-off</strong> antara jumlah fitur (Top 10 vs All Features) terhadap performa dan waktu training</li>
<li><strong>Menggunakan 5-Fold Cross Validation</strong> untuk evaluasi yang robust</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">1.3 Referensi Utama: Jurnal Prasad &amp; Chandra (2023)</h2><a id="user-content-13-referensi-utama-jurnal-prasad--chandra-2023" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 1.3 Referensi Utama: Jurnal Prasad &amp; Chandra (2023)" href="#13-referensi-utama-jurnal-prasad--chandra-2023"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Dataset yang digunakan berasal dari paper:</p>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><strong>"PhiUSIIL: A diverse security profile empowered phishing URL detection framework based on similarity index and incremental learning"</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Penulis:</strong> Arvind Prasad &amp; Shalini Chandra</li>
<li><strong>Jurnal:</strong> Computers &amp; Security (2023)</li>
<li><strong>DOI:</strong> <a href="https://doi.org/10.1016/j.cose.2023.103545" rel="nofollow">https://doi.org/10.1016/j.cose.2023.103545</a></li>
</ul>
</blockquote>
<p dir="auto">Dalam jurnal Prasad, mereka menggunakan:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Dataset:</strong> 235,795 URL (134,850 legitimate + 100,945 phishing)</li>
<li><strong>Fitur:</strong> 54-63 fitur yang diekstrak dari URL dan source code webpage</li>
<li><strong>Model:</strong> Random Forest, XGBoost, SVM, dan lainnya</li>
<li><strong>Evaluasi:</strong> Cross Validation dengan metrik Accuracy, Precision, Recall, F1-Score</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">2. DATASET PhiUSIIL</h1><a id="user-content-2-dataset-phiusiil" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 2. DATASET PhiUSIIL" href="#2-dataset-phiusiil"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">2.1 Informasi Dataset</h2><a id="user-content-21-informasi-dataset" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 2.1 Informasi Dataset" href="#21-informasi-dataset"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">2.2 Kategori Fitur</h2><a id="user-content-22-kategori-fitur" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 2.2 Kategori Fitur" href="#22-kategori-fitur"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Fitur dalam dataset dibagi menjadi beberapa kategori:</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">A. Fitur URL-Based (Berbasis URL)</h3><a id="user-content-a-fitur-url-based-berbasis-url" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: A. <p dir="auto"><strong>Alasan:</strong> XGBoost memerlukan OpenMP runtime yang tidak terinstall. <code>GradientBoostingClassifier</code> dari scikit-learn adalah alternatif yang equivalent karena keduanya menggunakan prinsip <strong>Gradient Boosting</strong>.</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Penjelasan:</h3><a id="user-content-penjelasan" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Penjelasan:" href="#penjelasan"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong><code>pd.read_csv()</code></strong>: Membaca file CSV ke dalam pandas DataFrame</li>
<li><strong><code>df.shape</code></strong>: Menampilkan dimensi data (rows, columns)</li>

</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">4.3 Cell 3: Data Preprocessing</h2><a id="user-content-43-cell-3-data-preprocessing" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 4.3 Cell 3: Data Preprocessing" href="#43-cell-3-data-preprocessing"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Kolom non-numerik yang harus di-drop
non_numeric_cols = ['FILENAME', 'URL', 'Domain', 'TLD', 'Title']

# Drop kolom non-numerik
df_numeric = df.drop(columns=non_numeric_cols, errors='ignore')

# Pisahkan fitur dan target
X = df_numeric.drop(columns=['label'])
y = df_numeric['label']

# Handle missing values
X = X.fillna(X.median())

# Pastikan semua kolom numerik
X = X.apply(pd.to_numeric, errors='coerce')
X = X.fillna(X.median())

print(f&quot;Features shape: {X.shape}&quot;)
print(f&quot;Target shape: {y.shape}&quot;)"><pre><span class="pl-c"># Kolom non-numerik yang harus di-drop</span>
<span class="pl-s1">non_numeric_cols</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> [<span class="pl-s">'FILENAME'</span>, <span class="pl-s">'URL'</span>, <span class="pl-s">'Domain'</span>, <span class="pl-s">'TLD'</span>, <span class="pl-s">'Title'</span>]

<span class="pl-c"># Drop kolom non-numerik</span>
<span class="pl-s1">df_numeric</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">df</span>.<span class="pl-c1">drop</span>(<span class="pl-s1">columns</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">non_numeric_cols</span>, <span class="pl-s1">errors</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'ignore'</span>)

<span class="pl-c"># Pisahkan fitur dan target</span>
<span class="pl-c1">X</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">df_numeric</span>.<span class="pl-c1">drop</span>(<span class="pl-s1">columns</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span>[<span class="pl-s">'label'</span>])
<span class="pl-s1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">df_numeric</span>[<span class="pl-s">'label'</span>]

<span class="pl-c"># Handle missing values</span>
<span class="pl-c1">X</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">X</span>.<span class="pl-c1">fillna</span>(<span class="pl-c1">X</span>.<span class="pl-c1">median</span>())

<span class="pl-c"># Pastikan semua kolom numerik</span>
<span class="pl-c1">X</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">X</span>.<span class="pl-c1">apply</span>(<span class="pl-s1">pd</span>.<span class="pl-c1">to_numeric</span>, <span class="pl-s1">errors</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'coerce'</span>)
<span class="pl-c1">X</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">X</span>.<span class="pl-c1">fillna</span>(<span class="pl-c1">X</span>.<span class="pl-c1">median</span>())

<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">f"Features shape: <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">X</span>.<span class="pl-c1">shape</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>"</span>)
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">f"Target shape: <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">y</span>.<span class="pl-c1">shape</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>"</span>)</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Penjelasan Detail:</h3><a id="user-content-penjelasan-detail" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Penjelasan Detail:" href="#penjelasan-detail"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Langkah 1: Drop Kolom Non-Numerik</h4><a id="user-content-langkah-1-drop-kolom-non-numerik" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Langkah 1: Drop Kolom Non-Numerik" href="#langkah-1-drop-kolom-non-numerik"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="non_numeric_cols = ['FILENAME', 'URL', 'Domain', 'TLD', 'Title']"><pre><span class="pl-s1">non_numeric_cols</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> [<span class="pl-s">'FILENAME'</span>, <span class="pl-s">'URL'</span>, <span class="pl-s">'Domain'</span>, <span class="pl-s">'TLD'</span>, <span class="pl-s">'Title'</span>]</pre></div>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Kolom</th>
<th>Alasan Di-drop</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>FILENAME</code></td>
<td>Identifier file, bukan fitur</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>URL</code></td>
<td>String URL asli, tidak bisa diproses langsung</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>Domain</code></td>
<td>String domain name</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>TLD</code></td>
<td>String Top Level Domain (.com, .org, dll)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>Title</code></td>
<td>String judul halaman web</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Alasan:</strong> Model machine learning membutuhkan input numerik. Kolom string/categorical ini sudah diekstrak menjadi fitur numerik lainnya.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Langkah 2: Handle Missing Values</h4><a id="user-content-langkah-2-handle-missing-values" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Langkah 2: Handle Missing Values" href="#langkah-2-handle-missing-values"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="X = X.fillna(X.median())"><pre><span class="pl-c1">X</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">X</span>.<span class="pl-c1">fillna</span>(<span class="pl-c1">X</span>.<span class="pl-c1">median</span>())</pre></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Metode:</strong> Mengisi nilai kosong dengan <strong>median</strong> kolom</li>
<li><strong>Alasan memilih median:</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Lebih robust terhadap outlier dibanding mean</li>
<li>Cocok untuk data dengan distribusi tidak normal</li>
<li>Menjaga integritas distribusi data</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Langkah 3: Konversi ke Numerik</h4><a id="user-content-langkah-3-konversi-ke-numerik" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Langkah 3: Konversi ke Numerik" href="#langkah-3-konversi-ke-numerik"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="X = X.apply(pd.to_numeric, errors='coerce')"><pre><span class="pl-c1">X</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">X</span>.<span class="pl-c1">apply</span>(<span class="pl-s1">pd</span>.<span class="pl-c1">to_numeric</span>, <span class="pl-s1">errors</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'coerce'</span>)</pre></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong><code>errors='coerce'</code></strong>: Mengubah nilai yang tidak bisa dikonversi menjadi NaN</li>
<li>Kemudian diisi lagi dengan median</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Hasil Preprocessing:</h3><a id="user-content-hasil-preprocessing" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Hasil Preprocessing:" href="#hasil-preprocessing"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Input:</strong> 59 kolom (termasuk label dan non-numerik)</li>
<li><strong>Output:</strong> 53 fitur numerik + 1 target variable</li>
</ul>
<hr>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Penjelasan:</h3><a id="user-content-penjelasan-1" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Penjelasan:" href="#penjelasan-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">4.6 Cell 6: Training Function dengan 5-Fold CV</h2><a id="user-content-46-cell-6-training-function-dengan-5-fold-cv" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 4.6 Cell 6: Training Function dengan 5-Fold CV" href="#46-cell-6-training-function-dengan-5-fold-cv"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="def train_and_evaluate_cv(X, y, model, model_name, n_splits=5):
    &quot;&quot;&quot;
    Train model dengan 5-Fold Stratified Cross Validation
    dan hitung metrics + training time
    &quot;&quot;&quot;
    # Setup 5-Fold Stratified Cross Validation
    skf = StratifiedKFold(n_splits=n_splits, shuffle=True, random_state=42)
    
    # Define scorers
    scorers = {
        'accuracy': make_scorer(accuracy_score),
        'precision': make_scorer(precision_score, average='binary'),
        'recall': make_scorer(recall_score, average='binary'),
        'f1': make_scorer(f1_score, average='binary')
    }
    
    # Start training timer
    start_time = time.time()
    
    # Perform cross validation
    cv_results = cross_validate(
        model, X, y, 
        cv=skf, 
        scoring=scorers,
        return_train_score=False,
        n_jobs=-1
    )
    
    # End training timer
    training_time = time.time() - start_time
    
    # Calculate mean metrics across all folds
    metrics = {
        'accuracy': cv_results['test_accuracy'].mean(),
        'accuracy_std': cv_results['test_accuracy'].std(),
        'precision': cv_results['test_precision'].mean(),
        'precision_std': cv_results['test_precision'].std(),
        'recall': cv_results['test_recall'].mean(),
        'recall_std': cv_results['test_recall'].std(),
        'f1': cv_results['test_f1'].mean(),
        'f1_std': cv_results['test_f1'].std(),
        'training_time': training_time
    }
    
    return metrics"><pre><span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">train_and_evaluate_cv</span>(<span class="pl-c1">X</span>, <span class="pl-s1">y</span>, <span class="pl-s1">model</span>, <span class="pl-s1">model_name</span>, <span class="pl-s1">n_splits</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">5</span>):
    <span class="pl-s">"""</span>
<span class="pl-s">    Train model dengan 5-Fold Stratified Cross Validation</span>
<span class="pl-s">    dan hitung metrics + training time</span>
<span class="pl-s">    """</span>
    <span class="pl-c"># Setup 5-Fold Stratified Cross Validation</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">skf</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">StratifiedKFold</span>(<span class="pl-s1">n_splits</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">n_splits</span>, <span class="pl-s1">shuffle</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">True</span>, <span class="pl-s1">random_state</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">42</span>)
    
    <span class="pl-c"># Define scorers</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">scorers</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> {
        <span class="pl-s">'accuracy'</span>: <span class="pl-en">make_scorer</span>(<span class="pl-s1">accuracy_score</span>),
        <span class="pl-s">'precision'</span>: <span class="pl-en">make_scorer</span>(<span class="pl-s1">precision_score</span>, <span class="pl-s1">average</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'binary'</span>),
        <span class="pl-s">'recall'</span>: <span class="pl-en">make_scorer</span>(<span class="pl-s1">recall_score</span>, <span class="pl-s1">average</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'binary'</span>),
        <span class="pl-s">'f1'</span>: <span class="pl-en">make_scorer</span>(<span class="pl-s1">f1_score</span>, <span class="pl-s1">average</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'binary'</span>)
    }
    
    <span class="pl-c"># Start training timer</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">start_time</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">time</span>.<span class="pl-c1">time</span>()
    
    <span class="pl-c"># Perform cross validation</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">cv_results</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">cross_validate</span>(
        <span class="pl-s1">model</span>, <span class="pl-c1">X</span>, <span class="pl-s1">y</span>, 
        <span class="pl-s1">cv</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">skf</span>, 
        <span class="pl-s1">scoring</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">scorers</span>,
        <span class="pl-s1">return_train_score</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">False</span>,
        <span class="pl-s1">n_jobs</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span>
    )
    
    <span class="pl-c"># End training timer</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">training_time</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">time</span>.<span class="pl-c1">time</span>() <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-s1">start_time</span>
    
    <span class="pl-c"># Calculate mean metrics across all folds</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">metrics</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> {
        <span class="pl-s">'accuracy'</span>: <span class="pl-s1">cv_results</span>[<span class="pl-s">'test_accuracy'</span>].<span class="pl-c1">mean</span>(),
        <span class="pl-s">'accuracy_std'</span>: <span class="pl-s1">cv_results</span>[<span class="pl-s">'test_accuracy'</span>].<span class="pl-c1">std</span>(),
        <span class="pl-s">'precision'</span>: <span class="pl-s1">cv_results</span>[<span class="pl-s">'test_precision'</span>].<span class="pl-c1">mean</span>(),
        <span class="pl-s">'precision_std'</span>: <span class="pl-s1">cv_results</span>[<span class="pl-s">'test_precision'</span>].<span class="pl-c1">std</span>(),
        <span class="pl-s">'recall'</span>: <span class="pl-s1">cv_results</span>[<span class="pl-s">'test_recall'</span>].<span class="pl-c1">mean</span>(),
        <span class="pl-s">'recall_std'</span>: <span class="pl-s1">cv_results</span>[<span class="pl-s">'test_recall'</span>].<span class="pl-c1">std</span>(),
        <span class="pl-s">'f1'</span>: <span class="pl-s1">cv_results</span>[<span class="pl-s">'test_f1'</span>].<span class="pl-c1">mean</span>(),
        <span class="pl-s">'f1_std'</span>: <span class="pl-s1">cv_results</span>[<span class="pl-s">'test_f1'</span>].<span class="pl-c1">std</span>(),
        <span class="pl-s">'training_time'</span>: <span class="pl-s1">training_time</span>
    }
    
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">metrics</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Penjelasan Detail:</h3><a id="user-content-penjelasan-detail-1" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Penjelasan Detail:" href="#penjelasan-detail-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Parameter StratifiedKFold:</h4><a id="user-content-parameter-stratifiedkfold" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Parameter StratifiedKFold:" href="#parameter-stratifiedkfold"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Parameter</th>
<th>Nilai</th>
<th>Penjelasan</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>n_splits=5</code></td>
<td>5</td>
<td>Membagi data menjadi 5 bagian (80% train, 20% test per fold)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>shuffle=True</code></td>
<td>True</td>
<td>Mengacak data sebelum split untuk menghindari bias urutan</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>random_state=42</code></td>
<td>42</td>
<td>Seed untuk reproducibility (hasil sama setiap kali dijalankan)</td>
</tr>
</tbody>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Mengapa Stratified?</h4><a id="user-content-mengapa-stratified" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Mengapa Stratified?" href="#mengapa-stratified"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Stratified</strong> memastikan <strong>proporsi kelas sama</strong> di setiap fold:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Legitimate (57.2%) : Phishing (42.8%) di setiap fold</li>
<li>Mencegah fold dengan mayoritas satu kelas saja</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Scorers yang Digunakan:</h4><a id="user-content-scorers-yang-digunakan" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Scorers yang Digunakan:" href="#scorers-yang-digunakan"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Metric</th>
<th>Formula</th>
<th>Interpretasi</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><strong>Accuracy</strong></td>
<td>(TP+TN)/(TP+TN+FP+FN)</td>
<td>Persentase prediksi benar dari total</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>Precision</strong></td>
<td>TP/(TP+FP)</td>
<td>Dari yang diprediksi positive, berapa yang benar</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>Recall</strong></td>
<td>TP/(TP+FN)</td>
<td>Dari yang actual positive, berapa yang terdeteksi</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>F1-Score</strong></td>
<td>2×(Precision×Recall)/(Precision+Recall)</td>
<td>Harmonic mean Precision &amp; Recall</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<p dir="auto">Keterangan:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>TP</strong> = True Positive (Benar mendeteksi legitimate)</li>
<li><strong>TN</strong> = True Negative (Benar mendeteksi phishing)</li>
<li><strong>FP</strong> = False Positive (Salah mendeteksi sebagai legitimate)</li>
<li><strong>FN</strong> = False Negative (Salah mendeteksi sebagai phishing)</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Parameter cross_validate:</h4><a id="user-content-parameter-cross_validate" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Parameter cross_validate:" href="#parameter-cross_validate"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Parameter</th>
<th>Nilai</th>
<th>Penjelasan</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>cv=skf</code></td>
<td>StratifiedKFold</td>
<td>Menggunakan stratified cross validation</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>scoring=scorers</code></td>
<td>dict</td>
<td>Multiple metrics sekaligus</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>return_train_score=False</code></td>
<td>False</td>
<td>Tidak menyimpan training score (hemat memori)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>n_jobs=-1</code></td>
<td>-1</td>
<td>Gunakan semua CPU cores (parallel processing)</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">4.7 Cell 7: Model Definitions</h2><a id="user-content-47-cell-7-model-definitions" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 4.7 Cell 7: Model Definitions" href="#47-cell-7-model-definitions"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="def get_models(n_features):
    &quot;&quot;&quot;
    Get models dengan max_depth yang disesuaikan dengan jumlah fitur
    &quot;&quot;&quot;
    if n_features &lt;= 10:
        max_depth = 10  # Untuk top 10 features
    else:
        max_depth = 20  # Untuk all features (53)
    
    return {
        'Random Forest': RandomForestClassifier(
            n_estimators=100, 
            max_depth=max_depth,
            random_state=42, 
            n_jobs=-1
        ),
        'XGBoost': GradientBoostingClassifier(
            n_estimators=100, 
            max_depth=min(max_depth, 10),
            random_state=42
        ),
        'SVM': SVC(
            kernel='rbf', 
            C=1.0,
            gamma='scale',
            random_state=42
        )
    }"><pre><span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">get_models</span>(<span class="pl-s1">n_features</span>):
    <span class="pl-s">"""</span>
<span class="pl-s">    Get models dengan max_depth yang disesuaikan dengan jumlah fitur</span>
<span class="pl-s">    """</span>
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">n_features</span> <span class="pl-c1">&lt;=</span> <span class="pl-c1">10</span>:
        <span class="pl-s1">max_depth</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">10</span>  <span class="pl-c"># Untuk top 10 features</span>
    <span class="pl-k">else</span>:
        <span class="pl-s1">max_depth</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">20</span>  <span class="pl-c"># Untuk all features (53)</span>
    
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> {
        <span class="pl-s">'Random Forest'</span>: <span class="pl-en">RandomForestClassifier</span>(
            <span class="pl-s1">n_estimators</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">100</span>, 
            <span class="pl-s1">max_depth</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">max_depth</span>,
            <span class="pl-s1">random_state</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">42</span>, 
            <span class="pl-s1">n_jobs</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span>
        ),
        <span class="pl-s">'XGBoost'</span>: <span class="pl-en">GradientBoostingClassifier</span>(
            <span class="pl-s1">n_estimators</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">100</span>, 
            <span class="pl-s1">max_depth</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-en">min</span>(<span class="pl-s1">max_depth</span>, <span class="pl-c1">10</span>),
            <span class="pl-s1">random_state</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">42</span>
        ),
        <span class="pl-s">'SVM'</span>: <span class="pl-en">SVC</span>(
            <span class="pl-s1">kernel</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'rbf'</span>, 
            <span class="pl-c1">C</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">1.0</span>,
            <span class="pl-s1">gamma</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'scale'</span>,
            <span class="pl-s1">random_state</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">42</span>
        )
    }</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Penjelasan Hyperparameter Per Model:</h3><a id="user-content-penjelasan-hyperparameter-per-model" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Penjelasan Hyperparameter Per Model:" href="#penjelasan-hyperparameter-per-model"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🌲 RANDOM FOREST</h3><a id="user-content--random-forest" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🌲 RANDOM FOREST" href="#-random-forest"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="RandomForestClassifier(
    n_estimators=100, 
    max_depth=10/20,
    random_state=42, 
    n_jobs=-1
)"><pre><span class="pl-en">RandomForestClassifier</span>(
    <span class="pl-s1">n_estimators</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">100</span>, 
    <span class="pl-s1">max_depth</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">10</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">20</span>,
    <span class="pl-s1">random_state</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">42</span>, 
    <span class="pl-s1">n_jobs</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span>
)</pre></div>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Parameter</th>
<th>Nilai</th>
<th>Penjelasan</th>
<th>Alasan Pemilihan</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>n_estimators</code></td>
<td>100</td>
<td>Jumlah decision trees dalam forest</td>
<td><strong>Standar industri.</strong> 100 trees memberikan keseimbangan antara akurasi dan waktu training. Lebih banyak trees = lebih baik, tapi diminishing returns setelah 100-200</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>max_depth</code></td>
<td>10 (top 10) / 20 (all)</td>
<td>Kedalaman maksimum setiap tree</td>
<td><strong>Adaptif berdasarkan fitur.</strong> 10 fitur → depth 10 cukup untuk capture patterns. 53 fitur → depth 20 agar trees bisa model kompleksitas lebih</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>random_state</code></td>
<td>42</td>
<td>Seed untuk random number generator</td>
<td><strong>Reproducibility.</strong> Hasil eksperimen dapat direproduksi</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>n_jobs</code></td>
<td>-1</td>
<td>Jumlah CPU cores</td>
<td><strong>Parallelization.</strong> -1 = gunakan semua cores untuk training lebih cepat</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Perbandingan dengan Jurnal Prasad:</h4><a id="user-content-perbandingan-dengan-jurnal-prasad" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Perbandingan dengan Jurnal Prasad:" href="#perbandingan-dengan-jurnal-prasad"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Dalam jurnal PhiUSIIL, Prasad menggunakan parameter serupa:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>n_estimators</code>: 100-200</li>
<li><code>max_depth</code>: Tidak dibatasi atau 10-20</li>
<li>Hasil: <strong>99%+ accuracy</strong></li>
</ul>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">📈 XGBOOST (GradientBoostingClassifier)</h3><a id="user-content--xgboost-gradientboostingclassifier" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 📈 XGBOOST (GradientBoostingClassifier)" href="#-xgboost-gradientboostingclassifier"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="GradientBoostingClassifier(
    n_estimators=100, 
    max_depth=10,
    random_state=42
)"><pre><span class="pl-en">GradientBoostingClassifier</span>(
    <span class="pl-s1">n_estimators</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">100</span>, 
    <span class="pl-s1">max_depth</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">10</span>,
    <span class="pl-s1">random_state</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">42</span>

<td><code>n_estimators</code></td>
<td>100</td>

<td><strong>Standar untuk gradient boosting.</strong> 100 iterasi cukup untuk konvergensi</td>

<td><code>max_depth</code></td>
<td>10</td>

</tr>

<td>42</td>
<td>Seed</td>
<td><strong>Reproducibility</strong></td>
</tr>
</tbody>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Mengapa max_depth Lebih Kecil?</h4><a id="user-content-mengapa-max_depth-lebih-kecil" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Mengapa max_depth Lebih Kecil?" href="#mengapa-max_depth-lebih-kecil"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Filosofi Boosting:</strong> Menggunakan banyak "weak learners" (trees dangkal) yang di-boost iteratif</li>
<li>Trees dalam lebih berisiko <strong>overfitting</strong></li>
<li>Berbeda dengan Random Forest yang menggunakan trees dalam dan averaging</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Catatan XGBoost vs GradientBoosting:</h4><a id="user-content-catatan-xgboost-vs-gradientboosting" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Catatan XGBoost vs GradientBoosting:" href="#catatan-xgboost-vs-gradientboosting"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🎯 SUPPORT VECTOR MACHINE (SVM)</h3><a id="user-content--support-vector-machine-svm" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🎯 SUPPORT VECTOR MACHINE (SVM)" href="#-support-vector-machine-svm"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="SVC(
    kernel='rbf', 
    C=1.0,
    gamma='scale',
    random_state=42
)"><pre><span class="pl-en">SVC</span>(
    <span class="pl-s1">kernel</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'rbf'</span>, 
    <span class="pl-c1">C</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">1.0</span>,
    <span class="pl-s1">gamma</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'scale'</span>,
    <span class="pl-s1">random_state</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">42</span>
)</pre></div>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Parameter</th>
<th>Nilai</th>
<th>Penjelasan</th>
<th>Alasan Pemilihan</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>kernel</code></td>
<td>'rbf'</td>
<td>Radial Basis Function kernel</td>
<td><strong>Paling populer.</strong> RBF bisa menangkap non-linear relationships. Implicit mapping ke infinite-dimensional space</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>C</code></td>
<td>1.0</td>
<td>Regularization parameter</td>
<td><strong>Default yang balanced.</strong> C tinggi = margin keras (risk overfitting). C rendah = margin lembut (risk underfitting). 1.0 adalah sweet spot</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>gamma</code></td>
<td>'scale'</td>
<td>Kernel coefficient</td>
<td><strong>Adaptive.</strong> 'scale' = 1/(n_features × X.var()). Menyesuaikan dengan jumlah fitur dan variance data</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>random_state</code></td>
<td>42</td>
<td>Seed</td>
<td><strong>Reproducibility</strong></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Penjelasan RBF Kernel:</h4><a id="user-content-penjelasan-rbf-kernel" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Penjelasan RBF Kernel:" href="#penjelasan-rbf-kernel"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><math-renderer class="js-display-math" style="display: block" data-run-id="231e17f887dd96cfdd6bff3246dff1dc">$$K(x, x') = \exp\left(-\gamma |x - x'|^2\right)$$</math-renderer></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Intuisi:</strong> Mengukur similarity berdasarkan jarak Euclidean</li>
<li><strong>Gamma tinggi:</strong> Decision boundary kompleks, mengikuti data points (overfitting risk)</li>
<li><strong>Gamma rendah:</strong> Decision boundary smooth (underfitting risk)</li>
<li><strong>'scale'</strong> otomatis menyesuaikan</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Perbandingan dengan Jurnal Prasad:</h4><a id="user-content-perbandingan-dengan-jurnal-prasad-1" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Perbandingan dengan Jurnal Prasad:" href="#perbandingan-dengan-jurnal-prasad-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Prasad menggunakan SVM dengan:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Kernel: RBF</li>
<li>C: 1.0 atau grid search</li>
<li>Gamma: 'scale' atau 'auto'</li>
<li>Hasil: <strong>~99% accuracy</strong></li>
</ul>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">4.8 Cell 8: Main Training Loop</h2><a id="user-content-48-cell-8-main-training-loop" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 4.8 Cell 8: Main Training Loop" href="#48-cell-8-main-training-loop"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="for fs_name, features in feature_sets.items():
    n_features = len(features)
    
    # Initialize result storage
    results['Accuracy'][fs_name] = {}
    results['Precision'][fs_name] = {}
    results['Recall'][fs_name] = {}
    results['F1'][fs_name] = {}
    results['Training Time'][fs_name] = {}
    
    # Select features
    X_fs = X[features]
    
    # Scale data
    scaler_fs = StandardScaler()
    X_fs_scaled = scaler_fs.fit_transform(X_fs)
    
    # Get models
    models = get_models(n_features)
    
    for model_name, model in models.items():
        # Train and evaluate
        metrics = train_and_evaluate_cv(
            X_fs_scaled, y, 
            model, model_name,
            n_splits=5
        )
        
        # Store results
        results['Accuracy'][fs_name][model_name] = metrics['accuracy']
        # ... (store other metrics)"><pre><span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">fs_name</span>, <span class="pl-s1">features</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">feature_sets</span>.<span class="pl-c1">items</span>():
    <span class="pl-s1">n_features</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">len</span>(<span class="pl-s1">features</span>)
    
    <span class="pl-c"># Initialize result storage</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">results</span>[<span class="pl-s">'Accuracy'</span>][<span class="pl-s1">fs_name</span>] <span class="pl-c1">=</span> {}
    <span class="pl-s1">results</span>[<span class="pl-s">'Precision'</span>][<span class="pl-s1">fs_name</span>] <span class="pl-c1">=</span> {}
    <span class="pl-s1">results</span>[<span class="pl-s">'Recall'</span>][<span class="pl-s1">fs_name</span>] <span class="pl-c1">=</span> {}
    <span class="pl-s1">results</span>[<span class="pl-s">'F1'</span>][<span class="pl-s1">fs_name</span>] <span class="pl-c1">=</span> {}
    <span class="pl-s1">results</span>[<span class="pl-s">'Training Time'</span>][<span class="pl-s1">fs_name</span>] <span class="pl-c1">=</span> {}
    
    <span class="pl-c"># Select features</span>
    <span class="pl-v">X_fs</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">X</span>[<span class="pl-s1">features</span>]
    
    <span class="pl-c"># Scale data</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">scaler_fs</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">StandardScaler</span>()
    <span class="pl-v">X_fs_scaled</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">scaler_fs</span>.<span class="pl-c1">fit_transform</span>(<span class="pl-v">X_fs</span>)
    
    <span class="pl-c"># Get models</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">models</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">get_models</span>(<span class="pl-s1">n_features</span>)
    
    <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">model_name</span>, <span class="pl-s1">model</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">models</span>.<span class="pl-c1">items</span>():
        <span class="pl-c"># Train and evaluate</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">metrics</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">train_and_evaluate_cv</span>(
            <span class="pl-v">X_fs_scaled</span>, <span class="pl-s1">y</span>, 
            <span class="pl-s1">model</span>, <span class="pl-s1">model_name</span>,
            <span class="pl-s1">n_splits</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">5</span>
        )
        
        <span class="pl-c"># Store results</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">results</span>[<span class="pl-s">'Accuracy'</span>][<span class="pl-s1">fs_name</span>][<span class="pl-s1">model_name</span>] <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">metrics</span>[<span class="pl-s">'accuracy'</span>]
        <span class="pl-c"># ... (store other metrics)</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Penjelasan StandardScaler:</h3><a id="user-content-penjelasan-standardscaler" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Penjelasan StandardScaler:" href="#penjelasan-standardscaler"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="scaler_fs = StandardScaler()
X_fs_scaled = scaler_fs.fit_transform(X_fs)"><pre><span class="pl-s1">scaler_fs</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">StandardScaler</span>()
<span class="pl-v">X_fs_scaled</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">scaler_fs</span>.<span class="pl-c1">fit_transform</span>(<span class="pl-v">X_fs</span>)</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Formula:</h4><a id="user-content-formula" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Formula:" href="#formula"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><math-renderer class="js-display-math" style="display: block" data-run-id="231e17f887dd96cfdd6bff3246dff1dc">$$z = \frac{x - \mu}{\sigma}$$</math-renderer></p>
<p dir="auto">Dimana:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="231e17f887dd96cfdd6bff3246dff1dc">$x$</math-renderer> = nilai original</li>
<li>
<math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="231e17f887dd96cfdd6bff3246dff1dc">$\mu$</math-renderer> = mean kolom</li>
<li>
<math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="231e17f887dd96cfdd6bff3246dff1dc">$\sigma$</math-renderer> = standard deviation kolom</li>
<li>
<math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="231e17f887dd96cfdd6bff3246dff1dc">$z$</math-renderer> = nilai ter-standardisasi</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Hasil:</h4><a id="user-content-hasil" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Hasil:" href="#hasil"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Mean</strong> setiap fitur = 0</li>
<li><strong>Standard deviation</strong> setiap fitur = 1</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Mengapa Scaling Penting?</h4><a id="user-content-mengapa-scaling-penting" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Mengapa Scaling Penting?" href="#mengapa-scaling-penting"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Model</th>
<th>Perlu Scaling?</th>
<th>Alasan</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><strong>SVM</strong></td>
<td>✅ WAJIB</td>
<td>Distance-based. Fitur dengan range besar akan mendominasi</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>Random Forest</strong></td>
<td>❌ Tidak wajib</td>
<td>Tree-based, split berdasarkan threshold, tidak terpengaruh skala</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>XGBoost</strong></td>
<td>❌ Tidak wajib</td>
<td>Tree-based seperti RF</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Keputusan:</strong> Tetap scaling semua model untuk <strong>konsistensi</strong> dan <strong>fairness</strong> perbandingan.</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5. METODE FEATURE SELECTION</h1><a id="user-content-5-metode-feature-selection" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5. <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.1 Overview 4 Metode</h2><a id="user-content-51-overview-4-metode" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.1 Overview 4 Metode" href="#51-overview-4-metode"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<th>Cara Kerja</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><strong>Boruta</strong></td>
<td>Wrapper</td>
<td>Membandingkan fitur dengan "shadow features" (random permutation)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>RFE</strong></td>
<td>Wrapper</td>
<td>Eliminasi fitur paling tidak penting secara iteratif</td>

</tr>

<td><strong>ContrastFS</strong></td>
<td>Hybrid</td>

</tr>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.2 BORUTA</h2><a id="user-content-52-boruta" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.2 BORUTA" href="#52-boruta"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Cara Kerja:</h3><a id="user-content-cara-kerja" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Cara Kerja:" href="#cara-kerja"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Buat shadow features:</strong> Duplikat semua fitur, acak nilainya</li>
<li><strong>Train Random Forest</strong> dengan fitur asli + shadow</li>
<li><strong>Bandingkan importance:</strong> Fitur asli harus lebih penting dari shadow terbaik</li>
<li><strong>Iterasi:</strong> Hapus shadow, ulangi sampai konvergen</li>
<li><strong>Hasil:</strong> Fitur yang konsisten lebih penting dari random → "All-relevant features"</li>
</ol>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.3 RFE (Recursive Feature Elimination)</h2><a id="user-content-53-rfe-recursive-feature-elimination" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.3 RFE (Recursive Feature Elimination)" href="#53-rfe-recursive-feature-elimination"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Cara Kerja:</h3><a id="user-content-cara-kerja-1" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Cara Kerja:" href="#cara-kerja-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Train model</strong> dengan semua fitur</li>
<li><strong>Ranking fitur</strong> berdasarkan importance</li>
<li><strong>Eliminasi fitur paling tidak penting</strong></li>
<li><strong>Ulangi</strong> sampai tersisa jumlah fitur yang diinginkan</li>
<li><strong>Hasil:</strong> Top-N fitur paling penting untuk model</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Top 10 RFE Features:</h3><a id="user-content-top-10-rfe-features" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Top 10 RFE Features:" href="#top-10-rfe-features"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
