<td>URL</td>
<td>Probabilitas karakter dalam URL</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>5</td>
<td><code>LetterRatioInURL</code></td>
<td>URL</td>
<td>Rasio huruf vs total karakter</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>6</td>
<td><code>SpacialCharRatioInURL</code></td>
<td>URL</td>
<td>Rasio karakter khusus</td>
</tr>
<tr>

<td>Content</td>
<td>Jumlah CSS files</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>8</td>
<td><code>URL_Profanity_Prob</code></td>
<td>URL</td>
<td>Probabilitas kata tidak pantas</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>9</td>
<td><code>URLLength</code></td>
<td>URL</td>
<td>Panjang URL (phishing sering panjang)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>10</td>

</tr>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.4 CORRELATION</h2><a id="user-content-54-correlation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.4 CORRELATION" href="#54-correlation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Cara Kerja:</h3><a id="user-content-cara-kerja-2" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Cara Kerja:" href="#cara-kerja-2"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Hitung korelasi</strong> setiap fitur dengan target (label)</li>
<li><strong>Ranking</strong> berdasarkan absolute correlation</li>
<li><strong>Pilih Top-N</strong> fitur dengan korelasi tertinggi</li>
<li><strong>Optional:</strong> Hapus fitur yang saling berkorelasi tinggi (multicollinearity)</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Rumus Pearson Correlation:</h3><a id="user-content-rumus-pearson-correlation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Rumus Pearson Correlation:" href="#rumus-pearson-correlation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><math-renderer class="js-display-math" style="display: block" data-run-id="231e17f887dd96cfdd6bff3246dff1dc">$$r = \frac{\sum(x_i - \bar{x})(y_i - \bar{y})}{\sqrt{\sum(x_i - \bar{x})^2 \sum(y_i - \bar{y})^2}}$$</math-renderer></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Top 10 Correlation Features:</h3><a id="user-content-top-10-correlation-features" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Top 10 Correlation Features:" href="#top-10-correlation-features"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5.5 CONTRASTFS</h2><a id="user-content-55-contrastfs" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.5 CONTRASTFS" href="#55-contrastfs"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Cara Kerja:</h3><a id="user-content-cara-kerja-3" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Cara Kerja:" href="#cara-kerja-3"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Contrast mining:</strong> Identifikasi fitur yang "membedakan" kelas</li>
<li><strong>Statistical tests:</strong> Uji signifikansi perbedaan</li>
<li><strong>Ranking:</strong> Kombinasi contrast score dan significance</li>
<li><strong>Hasil:</strong> Fitur yang paling "membedakan" legitimate vs phishing</li>
</ol>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">6. MODEL MACHINE LEARNING &amp; HYPERPARAMETER</h1><a id="user-content-6-model-machine-learning--hyperparameter" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 6. <tr>
<td><code>n_estimators=100</code></td>
<td>100 trees</td>
<td>✅ <strong>Sweet spot</strong> antara akurasi dan waktu. Studi menunjukkan &gt;100 diminishing returns</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>max_depth=10/20</code></td>
<td>Adaptif</td>
<td>✅ <strong>Sesuai kompleksitas.</strong> 10 fitur → depth 10. 53 fitur → depth 20 agar bisa explore semua kombinasi</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>random_state=42</code></td>
<td>Fixed seed</td>
<td>✅ <strong>Reproducibility</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>n_jobs=-1</code></td>
<td>All cores</td>
<td>✅ <strong>Parallel training</strong></td>
</tr>

<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="     ┌─────────┐    ┌─────────┐    ┌─────────┐         ┌─────────┐
     │ Tree 1  │───▶│ Tree 2  │───▶│ Tree 3  │──▶ ... ▶│Tree 100 │
     │(weak)   │    │(weak)   │    │(weak)   │         │(weak)   │
     └────┬────┘    └────┬────┘    └────┬────┘         └────┬────┘
          │              │              │                   │
          │   Residual   │   Residual   │                   │
          └──────────────┴──────────────┴───────────────────┘
                                    │
                           ┌────────▼────────┐
                           │   WEIGHTED SUM  │
                           │   = Final Pred  │
                           └─────────────────┘"><pre class="notranslate"><code>     ┌─────────┐    ┌─────────┐    ┌─────────┐         ┌─────────┐
     │ Tree 1  │───▶│ Tree 2  │───▶│ Tree 3  │──▶ ... ▶│Tree 100 │
     │(weak)   │    │(weak)   │    │(weak)   │         │(weak)   │
     └────┬────┘    └────┬────┘    └────┬────┘         └────┬────┘
          │              │              │                   │
          │   Residual   │   Residual   │                   │
          └──────────────┴──────────────┴───────────────────┘
                                    │
                           ┌────────▼────────┐
                           │   WEIGHTED SUM  │
                           │   = Final Pred  │
                           └─────────────────┘
</code></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Hyperparameter yang Dipilih:</h3><a id="user-content-hyperparameter-yang-dipilih-1" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Hyperparameter yang Dipilih:" href="#hyperparameter-yang-dipilih-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Mengapa Shallow Trees untuk Boosting?</h3><a id="user-content-mengapa-shallow-trees-untuk-boosting" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Mengapa Shallow Trees untuk Boosting?" href="#mengapa-shallow-trees-untuk-boosting"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Boosting <strong>sequential:</strong> Error tree sebelumnya diperbaiki tree berikutnya</li>
<li>Trees dalam → <strong>Overfitting</strong> pada satu iterasi</li>
<li>Trees dangkal → <strong>Generalization</strong> lebih baik</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Perbandingan dengan Jurnal Prasad:</h3><a id="user-content-perbandingan-dengan-jurnal-prasad-3" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Perbandingan dengan Jurnal Prasad:" href="#perbandingan-dengan-jurnal-prasad-3"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">6.3 Support Vector Machine (SVM)</h2><a id="user-content-63-support-vector-machine-svm" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 6.3 Support Vector Machine (SVM)" href="#63-support-vector-machine-svm"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Arsitektur SVM dengan RBF Kernel:</h3><a id="user-content-arsitektur-svm-dengan-rbf-kernel" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Arsitektur SVM dengan RBF Kernel:" href="#arsitektur-svm-dengan-rbf-kernel"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="                         HIGH-DIMENSIONAL SPACE
                         (via RBF kernel)
                         
    ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    │                      ○                            │
    │               ○    ○  ○                          │
    │            ○    LEGITIMATE                        │
    │               ○       ○                          │
    │                                                   │
    │   ════════════════════════════════════════════   │  ← HYPERPLANE
    │                                                   │
    │               ×           ×                       │
    │            ×    PHISHING    ×                    │
    │               ×    ×    ×                        │
    │                      ×                           │
    └───────────────────────────────────────────────────┘"><pre class="notranslate"><code>                         HIGH-DIMENSIONAL SPACE
                         (via RBF kernel)
                         
    ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    │                      ○                            │
    │               ○    ○  ○                          │
    │            ○    LEGITIMATE                        │
    │               ○       ○                          │
    │                                                   │
    │   ════════════════════════════════════════════   │  ← HYPERPLANE
    │                                                   │
    │               ×           ×                       │
    │            ×    PHISHING    ×                    │
    │               ×    ×    ×                        │
    │                      ×                           │
    └───────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
</code></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">RBF Kernel Formula:</h3><a id="user-content-rbf-kernel-formula" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: RBF Kernel Formula:" href="#rbf-kernel-formula"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><math-renderer class="js-display-math" style="display: block" data-run-id="231e17f887dd96cfdd6bff3246dff1dc">$$K(x_i, x_j) = \exp\left(-\gamma |x_i - x_j|^2\right)$$</math-renderer></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Hyperparameter yang Dipilih:</h3><a id="user-content-hyperparameter-yang-dipilih-2" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Hyperparameter yang Dipilih:" href="#hyperparameter-yang-dipilih-2"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Parameter</th>
<th>Nilai</th>
<th>Justifikasi</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>kernel='rbf'</code></td>
<td>RBF</td>
<td>✅ <strong>Paling versatile.</strong> Dapat menangkap non-linear patterns</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>C=1.0</code></td>
<td>Regularization</td>
<td>✅ <strong>Balanced.</strong> Tidak terlalu strict (overfitting) atau loose (underfitting)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>gamma='scale'</code></td>
<td>Auto-scaled</td>
<td>✅ <strong>Adaptive.</strong> = 1/(n_features × X.var()), menyesuaikan dengan data</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>random_state=42</code></td>
<td>Fixed seed</td>
<td>✅ <strong>Reproducibility</strong></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>

<p dir="auto"><strong>Proporsi kelas SAMA di setiap fold!</strong> Ini mencegah bias jika satu fold kebetulan memiliki lebih banyak kelas tertentu.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">7.3 Keuntungan 5-Fold CV:</h2><a id="user-content-73-keuntungan-5-fold-cv" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 7.3 Keuntungan 5-Fold CV:" href="#73-keuntungan-5-fold-cv"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Keuntungan</th>
<th>Penjelasan</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><strong>Robust evaluation</strong></td>
<td>Semua data digunakan untuk training DAN testing</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>Reduce variance</strong></td>
<td>Hasil tidak bergantung pada satu split</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>Better generalization estimate</strong></td>
<td>Lebih representatif dari performa sebenarnya</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>Detect overfitting</strong></td>
<td>Jika std tinggi → model tidak stabil</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">7.4 Mengapa 5 Fold (bukan 3 atau 10)?</h2><a id="user-content-74-mengapa-5-fold-bukan-3-atau-10" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 7.4 Mengapa 5 Fold (bukan 3 atau 10)?" href="#74-mengapa-5-fold-bukan-3-atau-10"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>K-Fold</th>
<th>Training Size</th>
<th>Bias</th>
<th>Variance</th>
<th>Waktu</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><strong>3-Fold</strong></td>
<td>66.7%</td>
<td>Tinggi</td>
<td>Rendah</td>
<td>Cepat</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>5-Fold</strong></td>
<td>80%</td>
<td>Sedang</td>
<td>Sedang</td>
<td>Sedang</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>10-Fold</strong></td>
<td>90%</td>
<td>Rendah</td>
<td>Tinggi</td>
<td>Lama</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<p dir="auto"><strong>5-Fold adalah sweet spot:</strong> Cukup data untuk training (80%), cukup folds untuk robust estimate, waktu training reasonable.</p>
<hr>

<p dir="auto"><strong>Mengapa RFE Terbaik?</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Wrapper method</strong> - menggunakan model untuk seleksi, bukan hanya statistik</li>
<li>Memilih fitur yang <strong>optimal untuk model spesifik</strong></li>
<li>Kombinasi fitur URL-based + Content-based yang balanced</li>
</ol>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🔍 Temuan 3: XGBoost Konsisten Terbaik</h3><a id="user-content--temuan-3-xgboost-konsisten-terbaik" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🔍 Temuan 3: XGBoost Konsisten Terbaik" href="#-temuan-3-xgboost-konsisten-terbaik"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<p dir="auto"><strong>Mengapa XGBoost Terbaik?</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Gradient boosting</strong> - koreksi error iteratif</li>
<li><strong>Regularization</strong> - mencegah overfitting</li>
<li>Handle fitur dengan berbagai skala dengan baik</li>
</ol>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🔍 Temuan 4: SVM Lambat untuk Correlation/ContrastFS Features</h3><a id="user-content--temuan-4-svm-lambat-untuk-correlationcontrastfs-features" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🔍 Temuan 4: SVM Lambat untuk Correlation/ContrastFS Features" href="#-temuan-4-svm-lambat-untuk-correlationcontrastfs-features"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

</tr>

<td>1511.37s</td>

</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Penyebab:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Correlation/ContrastFS memilih banyak <strong>binary features</strong> (0/1)</li>
<li>SVM dengan RBF kernel <strong>kurang efisien</strong> untuk data sparse binary</li>
<li>Banyak support vectors yang dibutuhkan</li>
</ul>
<hr>

</ol>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">10.1 Ringkasan Eksperimen</h2><a id="user-content-101-ringkasan-eksperimen" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 10.1 Ringkasan Eksperimen" href="#101-ringkasan-eksperimen"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Dataset:</strong> PhiUSIIL dengan 235,795 URL dan 53 fitur numerik</li>
<li><strong>Feature Selection:</strong> 4 metode (Boruta, RFE, Correlation, ContrastFS)</li>
<li><strong>Models:</strong> 3 classifier (Random Forest, XGBoost, SVM)</li>
<li><strong>Validation:</strong> 5-Fold Stratified Cross Validation</li>
<li><strong>Total Eksperimen:</strong> 15 kombinasi</li>
</ol>

<tr>
<th>No</th>
<th>Temuan</th>
<th>Implikasi</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>1</td>
<td>All Features = Akurasi tertinggi (99.92%)</td>
<td>Gunakan jika akurasi prioritas utama</td>

<td>2</td>
<td>RFE = Feature Selection terbaik</td>

<td>Feature selection sangat worth it</td>

<td>5</td>
<td>Random Forest = Paling cepat</td>
<td>10-30x lebih cepat dari SVM</td>
</tr>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">10.3 Best Practice untuk Phishing Detection</h2><a id="user-content-103-best-practice-untuk-phishing-detection" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 10.3 Best Practice untuk Phishing Detection" href="#103-best-practice-untuk-phishing-detection"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                   REKOMENDASI FINAL                             │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                                  │
│   🏆 PRODUKSI (High Accuracy):                                  │
│      → RFE Top 10 + XGBoost                                     │
│      → F1: 99.89%, Time: 200s                                   │
│                                                                  │
│   ⚡ REAL-TIME (Fast Inference):                                │
│      → RFE Top 10 + Random Forest                               │
│      → F1: 99.79%, Time: 34s                                    │
│                                                                  │
│   📊 RESEARCH (Maximum Accuracy):                               │
│      → All Features + XGBoost                                   │
│      → F1: 99.93%, Time: 500s                                   │
│                                                                  │

    <div id="js-global-screen-reader-notice-assertive" class="sr-only mt-n1" aria-live="assertive" aria-atomic="true"></div>
  </body>
</html>
